Update Order Totals: UPDATE OrderHeader WITH (ROWLOCK) SET SubTotal = SumPrice, OrderSurcharge = SumSurcharge, Discount = SumDiscount, ShipFee = 10, Total = SumPrice + SumSurcharge + 10 - SumDiscount FROM OrderHeader INNER JOIN (SELECT OrderLine.OrderNumber, SUM(Price) AS SumPrice, SUM(Surcharge) AS SumSurcharge, SUM(Discount) AS SumDiscount FROM OrderLine (NOLOCK) GROUP BY OrderLine.OrderNumber) AS OL ON OrderHeader.OrderNumber = OL.OrderNumber WHERE OrderHeader.IPAddress = 'AFB 2015' AND OrderHeader.StatusCode = 'R'
